</td></tr><tr style="display:none"><td colspan="2">
</td></tr><tr><td colspan="2" class="infobox-full-data"><link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1066479718"></td></tr><tr><th colspan="2" class="infobox-header" style="background-color: #b0c4de;">Korean name</th></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/Hangul" title="Hangul">Hangul</a></th><td class="infobox-data"><div style="display: inline; font-size: 1rem;"><span title="Korean-language text"><span lang="ko-Hang"><a href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/%EC%97%A0%EB%B2%84" class="extiw" title="wikt:엠버">엠버</a></span></span></div></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/Revised_Romanization_of_Korean" title="Revised Romanization of Korean">Revised Romanization</a></th><td class="infobox-data"><span title="Revised Romanization of Korean transliteration"><i lang="ko-Latn">Embeo</i></span></td></tr><tr><th scope="row" class="infobox-label" style="font-weight: normal;"><a href="/wiki/McCune%E2%80%93Reischauer" title="McCune–Reischauer">McCune–Reischauer</a></th><td class="infobox-data"><span title="McCune–Reischauer transliteration"><i lang="ko-Latn">Embŏ</i></span></td></tr><tr style="display:none"><td colspan="2">
</td></tr><tr><td colspan="2">
<div class="shortdescription nomobile noexcerpt noprint searchaux" style="display:none">Musical artist</div></td></tr></tbody></table>
<p><b>Amber Josephine Liu</b><sup id="cite_ref-Amber&#39;s_name_1-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Amber&#39;s_name-1">&#91;1&#93;</a></sup> (born September 18, 1992), also known mononymously as <b>Amber</b>, is an American<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2">&#91;2&#93;</a></sup> singer, rapper, and songwriter.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-3">&#91;3&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> She debuted as a member of the South Korean girl group <a href="/wiki/F(x)_(group)" class="mw-redirect" title="F(x) (group)">f(x)</a> in September 2009. In 2015, she became the first f(x) member to make a solo debut with the release of her first extended play <i><a href="/wiki/Beautiful_(Amber_EP)" class="mw-redirect" title="Beautiful (Amber EP)">Beautiful</a></i> and has since released solo singles in Korean, English, and Mandarin.
</p><p>In July 2018, she joined Steel Wool Entertainment following her original label <a href="/wiki/SM_Entertainment" title="SM Entertainment">SM Entertainment</a>’s joint partnership with Steel Wool to manage her American activities. In September 2019, she left SM and exclusively signed with Steel Wool prior to the release of her 2020 extended play <i>X.</i> In May 2021, she also signed with Ryce Entertainment for her activities in China following a successful stint as a mentor in survival show <i><a href="/wiki/Produce_Camp_2021" title="Produce Camp 2021">Produce Camp 2021</a></i>.
</p>
<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Life_and_career">Life and career</span></h2>
<h3><span id="1992.E2.80.932010:_Early_life_and_career_beginnings"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="1992–2010:_Early_life_and_career_beginnings">1992–2010: Early life and career beginnings</span></h3>
<p>Liu was born on September 18, 1992, in <a href="/wiki/Los_Angeles" title="Los Angeles">Los Angeles</a>, <a href="/wiki/California" title="California">California</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Her parents are from <a href="/wiki/Taiwan" title="Taiwan">Taiwan</a> and her father has <a href="/wiki/Teochew_people" title="Teochew people">Teochew</a> ancestry.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup> She has one older sister named Jackie.<sup id="cite_ref-r2_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-r2-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> She attended <a href="/wiki/El_Camino_Real_High_School" class="mw-redirect" title="El Camino Real High School">El Camino Real High School</a> in Los Angeles. Liu exceled in <a href="/wiki/SM_Entertainment" title="SM Entertainment">SM Entertainment</a>'s Los Angeles global audition in 2008 where she and one male were selected to be trainees for SM Entertainment. After a year and a half of training, she debuted as a member of the South Korean girl group <a href="/wiki/F(x)_(band)" class="mw-redirect" title="F(x) (band)">f(x)</a> in September 2009.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> During an episode of the group's reality show, <i><a href="/wiki/F(x)_(band)#2013:_South_by_Southwest,_Pink_Tape_and_the_first_concert" class="mw-redirect" title="F(x) (band)">Go f(x)</a></i>, Liu revealed that her parents initially had mixed feelings regarding her music career.  She stated: "My dad was very cautious, at first ...but then my mom was always supportive from the beginning. I really thank her and she also convinced my dad".<sup id="cite_ref-r2_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-r2-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<figure class="mw-halign-left" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Amber_Liu_in_Seoul_Plaza_(2).jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Amber_Liu_in_Seoul_Plaza_%282%29.jpg/197px-Amber_Liu_in_Seoul_Plaza_%282%29.jpg" decoding="async" width="197" height="251" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Amber_Liu_in_Seoul_Plaza_%282%29.jpg/296px-Amber_Liu_in_Seoul_Plaza_%282%29.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c0/Amber_Liu_in_Seoul_Plaza_%282%29.jpg/394px-Amber_Liu_in_Seoul_Plaza_%282%29.jpg 2x" data-file-width="436" data-file-height="555" /></a><figcaption>Amber performing at Seoul Plaza.</figcaption></figure>
<p>She has composed and written lyrics for some of the group's songs such as "Goodbye Summer" which was a single in their second studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/Pink_Tape_(f(x)_album)" title="Pink Tape (f(x) album)">Pink Tape</a></i>,<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup> and "Summer Lover" from their third studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/Red_Light_(f(x)_album)" title="Red Light (f(x) album)">Red Light</a></i>. Aside from featured songs, she also worked with fellow group mates <a href="/wiki/Luna_(South_Korean_singer)" title="Luna (South Korean singer)">Luna</a> and <a href="/wiki/Krystal_Jung" title="Krystal Jung">Krystal</a> for the <a href="/wiki/Original_soundtrack" class="mw-redirect" title="Original soundtrack">soundtrack</a> of <a href="/wiki/Korea_Broadcasting_System" class="mw-redirect" title="Korea Broadcasting System">KBS</a> drama <i><a href="/wiki/Master_of_Study" title="Master of Study">God of Study</a></i>, in a song called "Spread its Wings".
</p><p>She frequently collaborated with other SM Entertainment artists. Labelmate <a href="/wiki/Kwon_Yuri" class="mw-redirect" title="Kwon Yuri">Yuri</a> of <a href="/wiki/Girls%27_Generation" title="Girls&#39; Generation">Girls' Generation</a> performed a cover of <a href="/wiki/Ciara" title="Ciara">Ciara</a>'s song "<a href="/wiki/1,_2_Step" title="1, 2 Step">1, 2 Step</a>" at their first concert, <a href="/wiki/Into_the_New_World_(concert)" class="mw-redirect" title="Into the New World (concert)">Into the New World</a>, held on December 19 and 20, 2009 in <a href="/wiki/Seoul" title="Seoul">Seoul</a> and featured her as a rapper and dancer. The song was then included in their <a href="/wiki/Into_the_New_World_(album)" class="mw-redirect" title="Into the New World (album)">first live album</a>. In June 2010, she was featured in the lead single of Taiwanese singer <a href="/wiki/Danson_Tang" title="Danson Tang">Danson Tang</a>'s third Mandarin-language studio album, <i><a href="/wiki/The_First_Second" title="The First Second">The First Second</a></i>. She performed the Korean and English rap vocals and was also featured in the song's music video.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2011.E2.80.932014:_Television_roles"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2011–2014:_Television_roles">2011–2014: Television roles</span></h3>
<p>Liu has also started a career on television. From October 2011 to April 2012, she was part of the reality show <i><a href="/wiki/Invincible_Youth" title="Invincible Youth">Invincible Youth</a></i>. She had to leave the show to prepare for <a href="/wiki/F(x)_(group)" class="mw-redirect" title="F(x) (group)">f(x)</a>’s debut in Japan.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> In 2013, she was featured in the Korean version of the title track of <a href="/wiki/Henry_Lau" title="Henry Lau">Henry's</a>'s debut album, called "1-4-3 (I Love You)".<sup id="cite_ref-Nate.com_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Nate.com-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> She has hosted <a href="/wiki/Munhwa_Broadcasting_Corporation" title="Munhwa Broadcasting Corporation">MBC</a>'s music show <i><a href="/wiki/Show_Champion" title="Show Champion">Show Champion</a></i> with <a href="/wiki/T-ara" title="T-ara">T-ara</a>'s <a href="/wiki/Ham_Eun-jung" class="mw-redirect" title="Ham Eun-jung">Eunjung</a> for a year, both of them stepped down as hosts on December 18, 2013.<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup> On June 6, 2014, she became a host of the <a href="/wiki/Korean_Broadcasting_System" title="Korean Broadcasting System">KBS</a> show, <i>A Song for You</i> with <a href="/wiki/Kangin" title="Kangin">Kangin</a> of <a href="/wiki/Super_Junior" title="Super Junior">Super Junior</a> and <a href="/wiki/Yook_Sungjae" class="mw-redirect" title="Yook Sungjae">Yook Sungjae</a> of <a href="/wiki/BTOB" class="mw-redirect" title="BTOB">BTOB</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> She was also a host of <i><a href="/wiki/We_Got_Married" title="We Got Married">We Got Married</a> Global Edition</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> In the same year, she appeared in a 9-episode travel reality series, <i>One Fine Day</i>, with singer <a href="/wiki/Ailee" title="Ailee">Ailee</a>, who is a close friend of hers. The show, which aired on MBC Music, followed a vacation trip they took and was filmed on <a href="/wiki/Jeju_Island" title="Jeju Island">Jeju Island</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> On December 31, Liu was confirmed as a cast member for the second female soldier special of MBC's <i><a href="/wiki/Real_Man_(TV_series)" title="Real Man (TV series)">Real Men</a></i>.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2015.E2.80.932019:_Solo_debut"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2015–2019:_Solo_debut">2015–2019: Solo debut</span></h3>
<figure class="mw-default-size" typeof="mw:File/Thumb"><a href="/wiki/File:Amber_Liu_at_Jeju_K-Pop_Festival,_in_October_2015_02.jpg" class="mw-file-description"><img src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Amber_Liu_at_Jeju_K-Pop_Festival%2C_in_October_2015_02.jpg/220px-Amber_Liu_at_Jeju_K-Pop_Festival%2C_in_October_2015_02.jpg" decoding="async" width="220" height="330" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Amber_Liu_at_Jeju_K-Pop_Festival%2C_in_October_2015_02.jpg/330px-Amber_Liu_at_Jeju_K-Pop_Festival%2C_in_October_2015_02.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/40/Amber_Liu_at_Jeju_K-Pop_Festival%2C_in_October_2015_02.jpg/440px-Amber_Liu_at_Jeju_K-Pop_Festival%2C_in_October_2015_02.jpg 2x" data-file-width="2000" data-file-height="3000" /></a><figcaption>Amber Liu at the Jeju K-Pop Festival, in October 2015.</figcaption></figure>
<p>Liu officially debuted as a solo artist, releasing her debut EP, <i><a href="/wiki/Beautiful_(Amber_EP)" class="mw-redirect" title="Beautiful (Amber EP)">Beautiful</a></i>, on February 13, 2015. The title track, "Shake That Brass", featured Girls' Generation's <a href="/wiki/Kim_Tae-yeon" class="mw-redirect" title="Kim Tae-yeon">Taeyeon</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> A few days prior to the release of the album, a lyric video for the B-side track, "Beautiful", was released. The music video contained childhood photos of the singer, as well as photos since her debut as a member of f(x). Its lyrics tells the story of the difficulties she faced as she chased after her dreams of being an entertainer and how she liked herself the way she is.<sup id="cite_ref-20" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> <i>Beautiful</i> debuted at number two on <i>Billboard'</i>s World Albums chart and number 19 on <a href="/wiki/Top_Heatseekers" class="mw-redirect" title="Top Heatseekers">Heatseekers Albums</a>. According to Jeff Benjamin of <i><a href="/wiki/Billboard_K-Town" title="Billboard K-Town">Billboard K-Town</a></i>, this ranking shows Amber has a large international fanbase.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>As a part of the <a href="/wiki/SM_Station" title="SM Station">SM Station</a> project, Liu's solo single, "Borders", was released in March 2016. She participated in composing, lyrics writing and arrangement of the song. Written entirely in English, the hip hop track relates her childhood experiences and gives a message not to give up on oneself against life difficulties.<sup id="cite_ref-22" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Liu released the digital single, “On My Own" on May 18, 2016. On May 25, she released another digital single titled "Need to Feel Needed".<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup> On September 9, 2016, SM Entertainment published the official music video for "Breathe Again". This was Liu's first entirely English song and her first collaboration with Japanese DJ, Ksuke.<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup> On April 15, 2018, Liu released her first English-language solo mixtape, <i>Rogue Rouge</i>, with six songs, free on SoundCloud. She also released a music video for one track, "Closed Doors", on YouTube, with plans to release a total of six videos.<sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In July 2018, she signed with Steel Wool Entertainment and was also registered  by her real name. The agency represents and promotes her in the United States through singing, acting, as well as directing videos.<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Liu is also signed with <a href="/wiki/United_Talent_Agency" title="United Talent Agency">United Talent Agency</a> to represent her worldwide activities.<sup id="cite_ref-Amber_UTA_27-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Amber_UTA-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup> In September 2018, Liu released a single album <i>White Noise + Lost At Sea</i>, which includes two songs "White Noise" and "Lost At Sea".<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On September 1, 2019, Liu announced her departure from <a href="/wiki/SM_Entertainment" title="SM Entertainment">SM Entertainment</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> Five days later, she confirmed that she would continue forward with her Steel Wool Entertainment contract, and would release an album that she previously prepared with the label.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup> On September 12, Liu announced that she was releasing her second EP, <i>X</i>, with six tracks. It was later confirmed that she would drop one track each month until the album's release on January 10, 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-sep212019_31-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-sep212019-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span id="2020.E2.80.93present:_Post-SM_career_and_activities_in_China"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–present:_Post-SM_career_and_activities_in_China">2020–present: Post-SM career and activities in China</span></h3>
<p>On January 28, 2021, Liu was confirmed to be a mentor on the fourth season of the Chinese version of Produce 101, titled <i><a href="/wiki/Produce_Camp_2021" title="Produce Camp 2021">Produce Camp 2021</a></i>, which ran from February until April 2021 and formed the boy group <a href="/wiki/INTO1" class="mw-redirect" title="INTO1">INTO1</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup> On April 5, 2021, Liu announced her third extended play, <i>y?</i>. Soon after on April 8, 2021, Liu released two versions of her song "Neon": a Mandarin version that featured Chinese hip-hop artist Blow Fever, and an English version featuring <a href="/wiki/Peniel_Shin" title="Peniel Shin">Peniel</a> from <a href="/wiki/BtoB_(band)" title="BtoB (band)">BtoB</a> with two accompanying music videos that she co-directed.<sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> On April 29, 2021, Liu released two more singles from her album <i>y?</i>: the Mandarin version of "blue" featuring <a href="/wiki/MaSiWei" class="mw-redirect" title="MaSiWei">MaSiWei</a> from <a href="/wiki/Higher_Brothers" title="Higher Brothers">Higher Brothers</a>, and an English song called "Vegas"; along with music videos for each.<sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> On May 27, Liu and Steel Wool signed a partnership with Ryce Entertainment for her solo activities in China.<sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On September 21, 2021, Liu announced her fourth extended play <i>Z!</i>, with the first single "Paradise" being released on September 24, and the second single "Bad Decisions" being released on October 29.  It was released on February 25, 2022.
</p><p>As of 2023, Liu is participating in Ride The Wind 2023.
</p>
